Welcome to the Northeastern University
Academic Catalog and Student Handbook

Undergraduate Catalog (Full-Time Day Programs) 
College of Professional Studies Undergraduate Catalog  
Graduate Catalog
Student Handbook
Course Descriptions

Catalog information: The information in this catalog is effective fall 2024 through summer 2025. Students who enrolled in their programs prior to fall 2024 should consult previous versions of the Northeastern academic catalogs, their academic advisors, and/or their degree audit reports for their specific requirements. 
Handbook information: The Student Handbook contains information and resources about Northeastern University’s student academic and cocurricular life, conduct, and the responsibilities of students and the university to one another, as authorized by the president or the Board of Trustees. For information about other academic policies, academic programs, and degree requirements, please refer to the Academic Catalog.  For information about faculty rights and responsibilities or general personnel policies, benefits, and services, please refer to the University’s Policies, and related  procedural guides, as appropriate. The Student Handbook contains information current as of the date of publication; however, such information is not intended to be and should not be regarded to be contractual and is subject to change at the discretion of the university.
